               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT ShowInternalInfo THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT DimSetEntry1.FIND('-') THEN
                                      CurrReport.BREAK;
                                  END ELSE
                                    IF NOT Continue THEN
                                      CurrReport.BREAK;

                                  CLEAR(DimText);
                                  Continue := FALSE;
                                  REPEAT
                                    OldDimText := DimText;
                                    IF DimText = '' THEN
                                      DimText := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',DimSetEntry1."Dimension Code",DimSetEntry1."Dimension Value Code")
                                    ELSE
                                      DimText :=
                                        STRSUBSTNO(
                                          '%1, %2 %3',DimText,
                                          DimSetEntry1."Dimension Code",DimSetEntry1."Dimension Value Code");
                                    IF STRLEN(DimText) > MAXSTRLEN(OldDimText) THEN BEGIN
                                      DimText := OldDimText;
                                      Continue := TRUE;
                                      EXIT;
                                    END;
                                  UNTIL DimSetEntry1.NEXT = 0;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Sales Header }

    { 7551;3   ;DataItem;RoundLoop           ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;

                               MoreLines := SalesLine.FIND('+');
                                 bLastLineNo := SalesLine."Line No.";
                               WHILE MoreLines AND (SalesLine.Description = '') AND (SalesLine."Description 2" = '') AND
                                     (SalesLine."No." = '') AND (SalesLine.Quantity = 0) AND
                                     (SalesLine.Amount = 0)
                               DO BEGIN
                                 MoreLines := SalesLine.NEXT(-1) <> 0;
                                 //>>>>>> BCSYS - Blanks Lines
                                 bLastLineNo := SalesLine."Line No.";
                                 //<<<<<< BCSYS
                               END;

                               //>>>>>> BCSYS - Blanks Lines
                               bPositionCurseur := 0;
                               bPageNo := 1;
                               bReportAmount := 0;
                               bCountMainLines := 0;
                               bCountBlankLines := 0;
                               bLastPage := FALSE;
                               //<<<<<< BCSYS

                               IF NOT MoreLines THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SalesLine.SETRANGE("Line No.",0,SalesLine."Line No.");
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,SalesLine.COUNT);
                               CurrReport.CREATETOTALS(SalesLine."Line Amount",SalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount");
                             END;

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    SalesLine.FIND('-')

                                  LigneMontantTVA."VAT Identifier" := "Sales Line"."VAT Identifier";
                                  LigneMontantTVA.InsertLine;

                                  _MontantRem := _MontantRem+"Sales Line"."Inv. Discount Amount";
                                  _Montant := _Montant+"Sales Line".Amount;
                                  _MontantTTC := _MontantTTC+"Sales Line"."Amount Including VAT"-_MontantTTC*("Sales Header"."Payment Discount %"/100);
                                  //AB6.JME.002-->>

                                  IF SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item THEN
                                    IF NOT Item.GET(SalesLine."No.") THEN
                                      Item.INIT;

                                  IF DisplayAssemblyInformation THEN
                                    AsmInfoExistsForLine := SalesLine.AsmToOrderExists(AsmHeader);

                                  IF NOT "Sales Header"."Prices Including VAT" AND
                                     (SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLine."VAT Calculation Type"::"Full VAT")
                                  THEN
                                    SalesLine."Line Amount" := 0;

                                  IF (SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::"G/L Account") AND (NOT ShowInternalInfo) THEN
                                    "Sales Line"."No." := '';

                                  NNCSalesLineLineAmt += SalesLine."Line Amount";
                                  NNCSalesLineInvDiscAmt += SalesLine."Inv. Discount Amount";

                                  NNCTotalLCY := NNCSalesLineLineAmt - NNCSalesLineInvDiscAmt;

                                  NNCTotalExclVAT := NNCTotalLCY;
                                  NNCVATAmt := VATAmount;
                                  NNCTotalInclVAT := NNCTotalLCY - NNCVATAmt;

                                  NNCPmtDiscOnVAT := -VATDiscountAmount;

                                  NNCTotalInclVAT2 := TotalAmountInclVAT;

                                  NNCVATAmt2 := VATAmount;
                                  NNCTotalExclVAT2 := VATBaseAmount;

                                  //Calc net price
                                  NetPrice := SalesLine."Unit Price"* (1-(SalesLine."Line Discount %"/100));


                                  IF SalesLine.Type = SalesLine.Type::Item THEN
                                    IF NOT ShowItemLine4ShipCharge AND
                                       ("Sales Line"."No." = SalesSetup."Item No. for Shipping Charge") THEN BEGIN
                                      IF NOT(SalesLine."Line No." = bLastLineNo) THEN
                                        CurrReport.SKIP
                                      ELSE BEGIN
                                        HideLineItemShipCharge := TRUE;
                                        bDeplacerCurseur(-1);
                                      END;
                                      //<<<<<< BCSYS
                                    END;

                                  // ACBDU 110314D.BEGIN
                                  IF "Sales Line"."Vendor No. for EDI Sending" = '' THEN
                                    BEGIN
                                      PickInfoText := Text50000;
                                    END
                                  ELSE
                                    PickInfoText := '';
                                  // ACBDU 110314D.END

                                  //>>>>>> BCSYS - Blanks Lines
                                  // Avancer le curseur pour la ligne vente
                                  IF ShowPickInfo THEN
                                      bDeplacerCurseur(1);

                                  IF ShowShelf THEN
                                    bDeplacerCurseur(1);

                                  bDeplacerCurseur(1);
                                  //<<<<<< BCSYS
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                SalesLine.DELETEALL;
                              END;
                               }

               AutoFormatType=1;
               AutoFormatExpr="Sales Header"."Currency Code" }

    { 3591;4   ;DataItem;DimensionLoop2      ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=FILTER(1..));
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF NOT ShowInternalInfo THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               DimSetEntry2.SETRANGE("Dimension Set ID","Sales Line"."Dimension Set ID");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN BEGIN
                                    IF NOT DimSetEntry2.FINDSET THEN
                                      CurrReport.BREAK;
                                  END ELSE
                                    IF NOT Continue THEN
                                      CurrReport.BREAK;

                                  CLEAR(DimText);
                                  Continue := FALSE;
                                  REPEAT
                                    OldDimText := DimText;
                                    IF DimText = '' THEN
                                      DimText := STRSUBSTNO('%1 %2',DimSetEntry2."Dimension Code",DimSetEntry2."Dimension Value Code")
                                    ELSE
                                      DimText :=
                                        STRSUBSTNO(
                                          '%1, %2 %3',DimText,
                                          DimSetEntry2."Dimension Code",DimSetEntry2."Dimension Value Code");
                                    IF STRLEN(DimText) > MAXSTRLEN(OldDimText) THEN BEGIN
                                      DimText := OldDimText;
                                      Continue := TRUE;
                                      EXIT;
                                    END;
                                  UNTIL DimSetEntry2.NEXT = 0;

                                  //>>>>>> BCSYS - Blanks Lines
                                  bDeplacerCurseur(1);
                                  //<<<<<< BCSYS
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE InitializeRequest@1(NoOfCopiesFrom@1000 : Integer;ShowInternalInfoFrom@1001 : Boolean;ArchiveDocumentFrom@1002 : Boolean;LogInteractionFrom@1003 : Boolean;PrintFrom@1004 : Boolean;DisplayAsmInfo@1005 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      NoOfCopies := NoOfCopiesFrom;
      ShowInternalInfo := ShowInternalInfoFrom;
      ArchiveDocument := ArchiveDocumentFrom;
      LogInteraction := LogInteractionFrom;
      Print := PrintFrom;
      DisplayAssemblyInformation := DisplayAsmInfo;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetUnitOfMeasureDescr@2(UOMCode@1000 : Code[10]) : Text[10];
    VAR
      UnitOfMeasure@1001 : Record 204;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT UnitOfMeasure.GET(UOMCode) THEN
        EXIT(UOMCode);
      EXIT(UnitOfMeasure.Description);
    END;

    PROCEDURE BlanksForIndent@3() : Text[10];
    BEGIN
      EXIT(PADSTR('',2,' '));
    END;

    PROCEDURE bDeplacerCurseur@1000000026(_Pas@1000000000 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      // -- BCSYS --
      bPositionCurseur += _Pas;
      IF bPositionCurseur > bLignesParPage THEN BEGIN
        bPositionCurseur -= bLignesParPage;
        bPageNo += 1;
      END;
      // -- Fin BCSYS --
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      //>>>>>> BCSYS - Blanks Lines
      line 32
      //Max 38 lignes
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Shared Data1 as Object
Shared Data2 as Object

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer, Group as integer) as Object
if Group = 1 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1),Chr(177))))
End If
if Group = 2 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data2),Chr(177))))
End If

End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object,Group as integer)
  If Group = 1 and NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
      Data1 = NewData
  End If

  If Group = 2 and NewData &gt;  "" Then
      Data2 = NewData
  End If

  Return True
End Function
